   <script>
    function isStorageEnabled() {
 	try{
 		sessionStorage.setItem("test","value");
 		if(sessionStorage.getItem("test") == "value") {
 			sessionStorage.removeItem("test");
 			return true;
 		} else {
 			return false;
 		}
 	} catch(err) {
 		return false;
 	}
 }
 
 var hasStorage = isStorageEnabled();
 
 function getFromStorage(key) {
 	if(hasStorage) {
 		return sessionStorage.getItem(key);
 	}
 	var cookies = "; "+document.cookie;
 	var parts = cookies.split("; "+key+"=");
 	if(parts.length == 2) {
 		return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
 	} else {
 		return null;
 	}
 }
 
 
 function setToStorage(key, value) {
 	if(hasStorage) {
 		sessionStorage.setItem(key, value);
 		return;
 	}
 	document.cookie=key+"="+value+";path=/";
 }
 
 
 
 	
 	var browserBlacklist = [
 		/^(?:.*(?:MSIE)\s[4-9].*)$/,   									//regex for detecting IE versions <= 9
 		/^(?:.*Chrome\/(?:[1-3][0-9]).*)$/,								//regex for detecting Chrome versions <= 39
 		/^(?:.*Android\s(?:[1-3][0-9]).*)$/,							//regex for detecting Android versions <= 39
 		/^(?:.*Firefox\/(?:[3][0-4]|[1-2]).*)$/,						//regex for detecting Firefox versions <= 34
 		/^(?:.*(iPad|Macintosh).*(Version\/(?:[3-6]).*Safari\/).*)$/	//regex for detecting Safari versions <= 6
 	]
 	
 	//METHODS
 	function isUAAccepted(ua) {
 		console.log("User Agent: "+ua);
 		if(ua) {
 			for(reg in browserBlacklist) {
 				if(browserBlacklist[reg].test(ua)){
 					return false;
 				}
 			}
 		}
 		//save a flag to say the browser has been checked in local storage
 		setToStorage("colrs.ua","y");
 		return true;
 	}
 	
 	function areCookiesEnabled() 
 	{
 		var cookieEnabled = (navigator.cookieEnabled) ? true : false;
 		if (typeof navigator.cookieEnabled == "undefined" && !cookieEnabled)
 		{
 			document.cookie = "test";
 			cookieEnabled = (document.cookie.indexOf("test") != -1) ? true : false;
 		}
 		return cookieEnabled;
 	}
 	
 	
 	//IMPLEMENTATION
 	if(!areCookiesEnabled()) {
 		window.location.assign("https://shop.coles.com.au/online/COLRSNoCookieErrorView?catalogId=10576&langId=-1&storeId=20601");
 	}
 	
 	var previouslyChecked = getFromStorage("colrs.ua");
 	
 	if((getFromStorage("colrs.ua") == null) || (getFromStorage("colrs.ua") != "y")) {
 		if(window.history && history.pushState && isUAAccepted(navigator.userAgent)) {
 			//do nothing
 		} else {
 			document.getElementsByTagName("html")[0].className = document.getElementsByTagName("html")[0].className + " ng-hide";
 			window.location.assign("https://shop.coles.com.au/online/OldBrowserErrorView?catalogId=10576&langId=-1&storeId=20601");
 		}
 	}
   </script>

             <p data-ng-show="messageVM.displayCountdown">Trying again in <span data-ng-bind="messageVM.timeToRetry"></span></p>
             <p data-ng-hide="messageVM.displayCountdown">Retrying...</p>
             <div class="alert-buttons-wrapper">
 			    <button class="button"> 
 			        <svg focusable="false" class="icon icon-refresh" role="presentation" aria-hidden="true">

   <script id="/online/COLRSRetriableMessageTemplate?storeId=20201&amp;langId=-1&amp;requesttype=ajax" type="text/ng-template">
    <div class="alert" data-ng-class="{'is-visible':messagePanelVM.isVisible != null}"
 		data-colrs-trap-focus data-trap-is-hidden="!messagePanelVM.isVisible" data-trap-allows-external="true" >
      
      <div class="alert-wrapper" data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.isVisible">
      	<span class="arrow" data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.showArrow"></span>
      
         <div class="alert-content">
         	<svg focusable="false" class="icon {{messagePanelVM.messages.message.icon}}" data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.messages.message.icon" role="presentation" aria-hidden="true">
                 <use data-ng-attr-xlink:href="{{'#'+messagePanelVM.messages.message.icon}}" xlink:href=""/>
              </svg>
            	
          	<div class="accessibility">Start of alert</div>
          	
           	<p role="text" data-colrs-trap-initial data-colrs-trap-first>
            		<span class="accessibility-inline">
            			Alert.
 				</span>
            		<span>{{messagePanelVM.messages.message.title}}</span>
 	        </p>
             
             <p data-colrs-trap-last>{{messagePanelVM.messages.message.text}}</p>
             
             <div data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.isRetriable">
 	            <div data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.messages.message.retryTicks > 0 && !messagePanelVM.retryFailed && !messagePanelVM.retrying">
 		            <div>
 		            	<p role="text">Trying again in <strong data-ng-bind="messagePanelVM.messages.message.retryTicks"></strong>&nbsp;<span class="accessibility-inline">seconds</span></p>
 		            	<div class="alert-buttons-wrapper">
 						    <button class="button" data-ng-click="messagePanelVM.retry()"><svg focusable="false" class="icon icon-refresh" role="presentation" aria-hidden="true">
 						            <use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="#icon-refresh"></use>
 						        </svg>{{(messagePanelVM.messages.message.options.retry.text)?messagePanelVM.messages.message.options.retry.text:'Try again now'}}</button>
 						    <button class="button" data-ng-click="messagePanelVM.cancel()"><svg focusable="false" class="icon icon-cross" role="presentation" aria-hidden="true">
 						            <use xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xlink:href="#icon-cross"></use>
 						        </svg>{{(messagePanelVM.messages.message.options.cancel.text)?messagePanelVM.messages.message.options.cancel.text:'Give up'}}     
 						    </button>
 						</div>
 		            </div>
 	           	</div>
 	           	
 	            <div data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.retrying" aria-hidden="true">
 	            	<p class="alert-retry">Retrying<span aria-hidden="true">...</span></p>
 	           	</div>
 	           	<div data-ng-if="messagePanelVM.retryFailed" aria-hidden="true">
 	            	<p class="alert-retry">Retry failed</p>
 	            </div>
            	</div>
            	<div class="alert-buttons-wrapper" data-ng-hide="messagePanelVM.isRetriable">
          		<button class="button" data-ng-click="messagePanelVM.acknowledge(button.action)" 
          				data-ng-repeat="button in messagePanelVM.messages.message.buttons" data-colrs-trap-last>
          			{{(button.text)}}
          		</button>
          	</div>
          	<div class="accessibility">End of alert</div>
         </div>
     </div> 
 </div>
   </script>
